Guard Training Institute Recruiting Male and Female Students 154

Both the Jiangsu Second Prison Branch Prison and the Shanghai First Special District Court Guardhouse believe that the current number of guards is insufficient, and more need to be added to strengthen prison affairs. Furthermore, the position of guard is the first step for prison personnel, and the Ministry of Judicial Administration has previously issued a notice stipulating that the chief guard should be promoted from senior guards. Therefore, it is necessary to cultivate the knowledge of the guards to a considerable extent. Sun Xiong, the director of the branch prison and the director of the guardhouse, has now been approved by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court to establish a male and female guard training institute. In addition to the current male and female guards being allowed to enter the institute for training, a notice was issued on the 1st of this month to recruit ten male students and thirty female students. The age of the applicants should be between 25 and 40 years old, and they must have graduated from a junior elementary school or higher. The original deadline for registration was set for the 10th of this month, and the examination was scheduled to begin on the 16th. Now, Director Sun feels that the previously set timeframe is too short and is deeply concerned that students from other areas will not be able to arrive on time, so the registration deadline for female students has been extended to the 25th of this month, and the examination date for both male and female students has been changed to the 30th of this month. If the examination results are satisfactory and the applicant is admitted, they will enter the training institute to receive training under the guidance of the director. Classes will be held from 7 PM to 9 PM every afternoon, except for Sundays and designated holidays, and the training will last for three months. If the examination is passed, a diploma will be awarded. If selected to be a guard, the monthly salary will be from fourteen to twenty yuan. Those who are not selected will be listed as substitutes for future vacancies. Anyone who has received a lower-level education and is currently unemployed can quickly bring a photo and resume to register.

Doing All Sorts of Evil in Jingmen, Including Murder and Arson

Identified and Arrested After Search by Local Chamber of Commerce President

Yang Chunrong, also known as Yi Ronghua, the leader of the bandits in Jingmen County, Hubei Province, commanded thousands of bandits, with a formidable force, kidnapping for ransom, robbing homes, committing murder and arson, and doing all sorts of evil. The elite of the area were completely trampled, and the people hated him to the bone. Yang had no place to stand, so he fled to Shanghai alone. The Jingmen County Government sent a document to the Hubei Security Office, which forwarded a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government, requesting them to pay attention to the search and arrest. On the other hand, Xiao Gongfu, the president of the Chamber of Commerce, instructed Liu Jianfu to come to Shanghai to investigate Yang's whereabouts. On the 28th of last month, Liu found that Yang was living in Room 278 of the Shanghai New Hotel at No. 331 Hubei Road in the Public Concession. He reported to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Director Wen instructed the detectives, led by Gao Wansheng and Liu Shaoqing, to go to the address with Zhao Ziren, a Chinese detective from the Old Gate Police Station. They arrested Yang and sent him to the First Special District Court. Because it was necessary to inquire with the Hubei Provincial Security Office and the Jingmen Local Court, the court ordered an adjournment. Yesterday morning, Feng Shide, the head of the Criminal Court of the First Special Court, reopened the hearing. The court first handed over the reply telegram from the Security Office to the police lawyer Ru Baoyi for review and stated that the Jingmen County Local Court had not yet sent an official document to the court, so the case still needed to be postponed. Gao Wansheng of the Public Security Bureau declared, "The document from the Hubei Provincial Security Office only stated that Yang Chunrong had committed crimes such as kidnapping, murder, and arson and requested that he be handed over to the Public Security Bureau for transfer. However, the wording was vague, without specifying who made the accusation, what kind of case was committed, and it did not conform to the agreement with this court. The Municipal Public Security Bureau should telegraph to inquire about the details of the case and the names of the victims. After receiving a reply telegram, we will verify the information." On one hand, this court will re-telegraph the Jingmen Local Court to investigate. The court ordered the case to be adjourned for verification.

—Splits Open Corpse Coffin; Chops Off Corpse Head; Strips Corpse Clothes—

Public Health Bureau Strictly Prevents Impostors: A Notice to Inform Citizens 168

The Shanghai Municipal Public Health Bureau hereby issues the following notice:

Regarding the registration and licensing of various professions related to public health, which are handled by this Bureau, all procedures are established according to regulations, and the fees to be collected are clearly specified. All revenue is deposited into the city treasury and official receipts stamped by the Finance Bureau are used as proof. All applications for registration and licensing are processed if they do not violate regulations, and are never deliberately obstructed. Even if there are shortcomings, guidance for improvement will be provided for re-processing. Any compulsory actions are always carried out by requesting the Public Security Bureau to order the relevant district offices to cooperate in enforcement, acting impartially according to regulations. Bribes are strictly forbidden and intercession is not permitted. This is the unwavering principle of this Bureau. However, it has come to our attention that some unscrupulous individuals are impersonating Bureau personnel, swindling and deceiving, attempting to defraud, or extorting money to satisfy their own desires, or soliciting license applications for personal gain. We have heard of such incidents repeatedly, and have been investigating and apprehending the perpetrators without success. Recently, one person was apprehended in the Zhabei area. In addition to detaining and severely punishing this individual, we will continue to investigate and apprehend others at any time. Fearing that citizens may be easily deceived by these illegal activities, we hereby issue this notice, urging you to pay attention to the following points:

1. Anyone who needs to apply for a license from this Bureau should come to the Bureau in person or apply in writing. If you encounter someone soliciting services on your behalf, you should refuse immediately to prevent them from profiting at your expense, causing you losses, and harming the Bureau's reputation.

2. Illegal fees are unlawful gains. This Bureau strictly prohibits all staff from using their position to demand anything, such as monthly allowances, holiday gifts, transportation money, or money for wine, shoes, and socks. All improper gains are prohibited. Do not attempt to offer such things, as it will harm both yourself and others.

3. If you believe there is an event that endangers public health, you can report it to the Bureau in writing for investigation and handling. If it is impossible to verify the facts after the event, you can report it to the nearest police post.

4. When encountering someone claiming to be conducting an official inquiry, you may ask to see their employee identification card (which must have their photo attached, indicating their title, name, and bearing the official seal). Health inspectors must wear uniforms and badges (stating their name and bearing the Bureau seal). You can also ask to see these to prevent impersonation.

We urge you to pay close attention to the above points. This is of utmost importance. This notice is hereby issued for public information.

April 12th, Year 22 of the Republic of China

Director Li Ting'an

Seven Families Scammed

Residents Should Be Extra Vigilant

Recently, four or five flamboyant women, dressed in black sheepskin coats and yellow overcoats, around thirty years old, speaking with a Hangzhou accent, have been loitering on the Bund, making a living by scamming people. A few days ago, students from the Nanyang Model High School in Xujiahui, Yang Shuguo, Xie Shixiao, Jin Yongguang, Wu Huaqing, Yao Yongyao, Zhu Zemin, and Jiang Baoshan, were at home during their spring break when these unemployed women visited, claiming to be the older sisters or relatives of certain students. The students, feeling strongly about their classmates, readily offered assistance. However, yesterday, when the school reopened and the students returned to class, they inquired about the truth from the classmates in question, who said that there was no such thing. This caused them to be shocked. As a result, seven people were scammed out of over one hundred dollars. Detectives have been dispatched to conduct a thorough investigation and apprehension. The addresses of those who were scammed are listed below: Yang Shuguo, residing at Hejiajiao, South of Fahua; Jin Yongguang, residing at West Qiaojia Road, inside the Dananmen; Wu Huaqing, residing on Ningbo Road; Yao Yongyao, residing on Seward Road; Zhu Zemin, residing on Shanhai Pass Road; Jiang Baoshan, residing at the end of Connaught Road, Singapore Road. According to student Yang Shuguo, classmates Ye Fuzeng, Xue Jinshou, Qiu Kunde, and Xie Dexian were also nearly swindled out of money and goods by the women. Those staying at home should be especially vigilant and on guard, so as not to be fooled.

City News 172

China Soap Company Celebration Banquet. The China Soap Company, located at No. 18 the Bund, Shanghai, has a prosperous business. Its products, such as Lux Soap, Sunlight Soap, and Xiangcheng Soap, are well-known. This spring, the company introduced a new goods-for-coupon system, and the drawing was held on the 12th. At 2 PM, the drawing took place at the company's soap factory in Yangshupu. Managers from various districts and foreign guests were invited to supervise. After the drawing, the guests were accompanied on a tour of the factory, and they admired the perfection of the internal equipment. That evening, a spring business celebration banquet was held at Yipinxiang, attracting a large crowd. Before the banquet, Mr. Robesen, the general manager of the company, gave a speech and awarded prizes. Among the district business comparisons, Mr. Qi Huichang, manager of the Shanghai district, achieved the best results and won a large silver shield. Mr. Chen Shanqing of the Haimen Department of Jiangsu Province won the personal championship. The other five winners, Li Zhiqin, Chen Liangfu, Zhu Xiulin, Wang Daren, and Zhang Zihe, each received a silver cigarette case.

Xuyuan to Be Transformed into Amusement Park. Xuyuan, located on Connaught Road in West Shanghai, is the most famous private garden in Shanghai. It has been established for over 20 years. The internal architecture includes various flowers and trees, as well as pavilions, terraces, and quadrangles. It is grand in scale and usually used for festive occasions. However, many people buy tickets to visit during the hot summer months. Recently, the owner of the garden, to provide social convenience for people to cool off in the summer, plans to open the garden to the public, collect various noble amusements, and build an open-air cinema, a golf course, a dance hall, and a billiard room in the garden. It is expected to open around the time of the Dragon Boat Festival.

Record of Lie Feng Silk Factory's Banquet. To promote domestic products and save the silk industry, the Lie Feng Silk Factory invited managers from Shanghai Guohuo, China Guohuo, Sincere, Wing On, New World, and other companies, as well as managers from Lao Jie Fu and other silk shops, to a banquet at the Dadong Restaurant yesterday to discuss solutions. More than 100 people attended. First, Xu Peikun, manager of Lie Feng, explained in detail how the factory had carefully improved its products and invented silk fabrics such as Wild Goose Feather, Bi He, and Diao Chan crepe, which were superior to imported products and were popular for a time. Recently, some people have engaged in unwarranted dumping, which has disrupted the market and affected the livelihoods of workers. He requested support. Wu Zhihao said that promoting domestic products is a way to resist foreign goods. The silk industry has a history of over 4,000 years, but it has declined due to a lack of unity. He hoped that the industry would unite to save the situation. Zhang Zilian said that he hoped the silk shops would share their experiences with the factories to improve production, and that they would encourage customers to use domestic products to benefit the people. As a result, everyone agreed that the silk industry has declined sharply in recent years, causing many people to lose their jobs in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. They were determined to unite, not to engage in infighting, and to save the industry.

Publishing World 173

Nanjing University. The agricultural books published by the Department of Agricultural Economics of Nanjing University have always been highly regarded by scholars. Recently, Mr. Zhang Xinyi has written "An Estimate of the General Situation of Chinese Agriculture," which includes 11 statistical tables and 12 statistical maps, detailing the number of farm households, population, land, and the area and yield of more than 20 major crops in 25 provinces of China. The price is two yuan. It is truly an essential reference for agricultural researchers and libraries. It is now exclusively distributed by the Author's Publishing House at 556 Fuzhou Road, Shanghai. The company is well-known for its promotional abilities, and is praised by writers in general, so they are happy to entrust their works to the company for exclusive distribution.

"Essential Knowledge for People in Wartime" is Republished. The Shanghai Weekly Press, due to the deepening threat of bandits and the urgent national crisis, believed that the Chinese people were at risk of being subjected to war anytime, anywhere. They realized that the Chinese people lacked knowledge of wartime matters. Recalling the January 28th Incident, the number of fellow countrymen who died was hard to count. They then collected all kinds of knowledge related to wartime and compiled the book "Essential Knowledge for People in Wartime." The first edition of 10,000 copies was sold out. It has now been reprinted with 50,000 copies. For the sake of widespread publicity, the company only charges the cost of five cents per copy. If organizations and schools purchase more than 100 copies for distribution, the company is willing to sacrifice freight costs or provide assistance.

The first three issues were bestsellers at home and abroad, and subscriptions came in droves. The first two issues have already sold out. The price is evident. The fourth issue was published the day before yesterday. The number of pages is only about ten fewer than a special issue, but the price is only five cents. The content is also very exciting, with steel and zinc plate illustrations, specialized treatises, and architectural regulations and contracts. People in the architectural industry and those intending to build houses should each have a copy. The distribution office of the journal is located at the Shanghai Architecture Association Monthly Department, Room 620, 6th Floor, Dalu Department Store, Nanjing Road, Shanghai. Each copy sells for five cents. For mail orders outside Shanghai, add five cents for postage; for mail orders within Shanghai, add two cents for postage. The annual subscription price is five yuan, with postage of 24 cents for local orders and 60 cents for out-of-town orders.

New Contribution to Women's Health. The greatest influence on women's health is menstruation. According to accurate statistics from famous European doctors, eight or nine out of ten women's diseases are due to menstrual irregularities. This number is alarming enough. Chinese women often avoid discussing this disease, and its impact on their health is immeasurable. It has recently come to our attention that Dr. Bi Fengzhang of Shanghai has specially compiled a book called "Women's Health Guide," which is being given to women. The book describes the causes, symptoms, and treatments of menstrual irregularities in detail. All women can send a letter to Shanghai P.O. Box 840 to request a copy.

Reader's Advisor

Regarding a Collection of Letters Discussing the Question of "Can We Return to the Countryside?" 177

(6) Letter from Mr. Hu Nianzhu of this city: I come from the countryside

I saw the discussion about going to the countryside in your column, which evoked my memories because I am just a country bumpkin from the countryside. My family, though not landlords, could still be considered grain rentiers. My family has a village estate with good waterways, fertile land, far from major villages, not connected to main roads, located in Shanggao County, a very undeveloped area in Jiangxi. Moreover, this estate is not in poor valleys and deep mountains, never visited by soldiers or bandits, and with no danger of harboring bandits. What a peaceful place! I originally had a plan to build an ideal rural village here, but I encountered difficulties as soon as I started. Someone like me, who has never been exposed to the sun, what skills do I have to deal with these dozens of acres of land? Hire a farmhand? You need to know that in the countryside, if you want to hire a teacher, you only need to say a word, and someone will recommend one from here or there. But if you want a long-term worker, it is indeed a bit troublesome. Needless to say, the usual practice is to pay half a year or a year's wages in advance. If they are good, they won't cause you to lose money. If they are not good, they might take on work for three or four landlords at the same time, or they might run away after working for half a year, or even before starting work. To be honest, it is almost impossible to be an idler in the countryside! The strange phenomena in the countryside are very worthy of our attention. On one hand, the population is rapidly decreasing; on the other hand, the amount of wasteland is increasing day by day. At the same time, on the other hand, a large number of vagrants are being produced. This contradictory phenomenon is obviously not just about the tillers not owning their land, but about owning land but not being able to till it. On one hand, there is the endless addition of exorbitant taxes and levies, but the biggest fundamental reason is due to the encroachment of foreign capitalism into the countryside, which has increased the level of rural life. At the same time, the prices of agricultural products have relatively decreased, especially in the last year or two. This has led to the bankruptcy of the rural economy, and many farmers have become soldiers and bandits. Naturally, these displaced farmers are not only transformed from producers into non-producers, but also from child-bearers into non-child-bearers, thus affecting the tragedy of abandoning baby girls, which is becoming more and more intense. If this continues, China's 400 million compatriots may not need the Japanese to trouble themselves! Editor, you are like an experienced self-cultivating farmer, even you have a crisis and the possibility of bankruptcy in the countryside. How can people who are used to city life make a living in the countryside? Mr. You Huaigao, please enlighten me. People in the city are forced to a dead end and want to go to the countryside; people in the countryside are forced to a dead end and want to go to the city. Where is the broad road? Also, can the economic bankruptcy and rural unrest caused by the relative decrease in agricultural product prices, the rapid increase in rural living standards, and the endless addition of exorbitant taxes and levies be remedied by rural education?

(7) Letter from Mr. Zhu Ying of this city: Under the current situation, going back to the countryside is practically impossible

The reporter introduced Mr. You Huaigao, saying: "Mr. You advocates rural education to save the country. He has done a lot of research on rural education and is also a practitioner." Indeed, after reading his reply to Mr. Xiongsheng's letter, his detailed and practical methods are beyond what empty theorists can utter. However, Mr. You said: "With my ability, I will spend ten years to build a new-style Arcadia in my imagination." Who doesn't dream of such a new-style Arcadia, who doesn't want to realize it immediately? Unfortunately, in China today, the entire rural economy is bankrupt, and people are struggling to survive. Where is there any extra strength to allow others to operate for a long time? Moreover, the resulting confrontation between two forces, which is already very obvious in some places, and though not very obvious in some places, is also advancing secretly in the undercurrent, these situations are difficult problems to deal with in the countryside. For example, according to Mr. You's method, if you return to the countryside and run such a school, which side will you take in the confrontation between the two forces? Taking the side of the powerful seems not to be the purpose of running a school; taking the side of the powerless will definitely be oppressed by the powerful. As for saying that you don't have any relationship with either side, that conflicts with Mr. You's so-called "spreading goodwill in the village"; and it is also absolutely impossible in reality. Although the countryside in the Jiangzhe area is relatively better in some places at present, after two or three years of invasion by imperialists and the gradual exploitation by domestic evil forces, won't it end up with the same fate! Therefore, it is probably impossible to build a new-style Arcadia in any part of China within ten years. Therefore, if Mr. Xiongsheng returns to the countryside, I am afraid that not only will he not achieve his lofty goals, but even his kind of "no courage to break the law, no courage to commit suicide" factor (the problem of livelihood) will still not be eliminated. Mr. You is a person who studies education, or perhaps he has a different vision for this field, we cannot know, I hope to be enlightened!

Education News 178

Important News

Declaration of the Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Education Association 179

Implement Wartime Education

Overall Air Force Plan

Monthly Allocation of Funds

The 12th Congress of the Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Education Association was held at Wuxi Normal School at the beginning of this month. Its proposals have already been published. The declaration of the association is as follows:

In the Franco-Prussian War, Germany became a superpower with one battle. Observers did not attribute it to the generals and soldiers at the front, but to the teachers in the schools. German Chancellor Bismarck said, "The power of one teacher is greater than that of 100,000 Mausers." The Japanese learned from this, and in the Russo-Japanese War, the whole country embraced a common hatred of the enemy, and they also became a superpower with one battle. Looking back at our country, the invaders are deep, and the situation is urgent. The four northeastern provinces have fallen under the iron hooves of the Japanese, and there is a growing tendency to cross the Great Wall and let their horses drink in the Yellow River to the south. The rivers and mountains are shrinking day by day, and the country is almost no longer a country. We, who are shamelessly occupying the ranks of secondary school teachers, dare not lag behind others in avenging our enemies. Since we have not served on the battlefield, we should devote our efforts to the lecture hall. We believe that the decline of the country is due to many reasons, such as the weakness of the people's patriotic concepts, due to the thinness of national consciousness, the lack of national defense, the incompleteness of military preparations, due to the lack of manufacturing, the lack of talent, and the daily urgency of the people's livelihoods, due to the lack of industrial and commercial prosperity, which is also due to the lack of scientific precision. After decades of education, learning has not been able to be applied, so we believe that today's education has the following three points: (1) We must arouse a strong national consciousness, so that young people can clearly understand where integrity lies; (2) We must improve the level of various disciplines, and instill in young people as much practical and useful scientific knowledge as possible, so that what they learn is practical and becomes the foundation of China's production education; (3) We must pay attention to military training, and cultivate young people's simple, hardworking, disciplined, organized, firm, and brave spirit. Today is a very special period for our country, and we should implement a very special education, in other words, wartime education, education for national salvation. All our facilities today must be based on our lifeline as the starting point. The above three points are the education for a very special period, the education for national salvation. We carefully endure the pain and propose it as a preparation for the rear support of the soldiers at the front, which is our view on education.

Since the war at the front is urgent, and the people have a patriotic enthusiasm, there have been donations from all sides to purchase aircraft. My colleagues dare not lag behind others in patriotism. Therefore, it was decided at this congress that, starting from this month, we will donate a percentage of our salary and deposit it in the bank, designated as a special savings fund for the development of China's air force. The intention is not just to provide a drop in the bucket, because the amount is very small, and we are not able to purchase aircraft for a while. But in fact, we are not yet clear to what extent our people are preparing for the country's air defense. We do not want to repeat the mistake of the 300 aircraft in the Northeast, which were used by the enemy. We deeply hope that the government and society will pay attention to the overall problem of the Chinese Air Force, and have a thorough solution, such as the cultivation of aviation talents, the manufacture of aircraft, and the plans for air defense in various places. We are willing for everyone to have savings for the development of a special air force fund, and at the same time hope that the government will realize the above thorough solution. In this way, we can achieve the practical effect of resisting Japan and saving the country. This is by no means a pedantic talk, and we are willing to share this concern with the people of the country. This is our view on donating our salary to save the country.

Education is the fundamental economy for saving the country, and funding is the lifeline of education. For five years of the European War, the sound of learning never stopped. The details of Jiangsu's education funding are probably not known to outsiders. The salaries of colleagues are in arrears for four months. The Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office is an agency in charge of special education funds. It has just released the funding for December. The lives of teachers and staff are deeply painful, and school facilities cannot be developed, all suffering from the impact of insufficient education funding. My colleagues, in order to prepare for the wartime education in this extraordinary period, also have to discuss education funding. We deeply understand that the administrative authorities and people from all walks of life pay attention to the importance of funding, take responsibility for their positions, and allocate funds on a monthly basis without further delays, so that teachers and staff do not have to worry about a lack of supplies, then when my colleagues devote themselves to the lecture hall, it is no different from serving on the battlefield, which is our view on education funding.

My colleagues, at the time of bright spring, used the rest of the spring break to gather in Wuxi to discuss education issues and draw up guidelines for the future. I hope that all parties will correct us, which would be a great blessing. This is our declaration.

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Announces Graduation Examination Methods for Primary and Secondary Schools 186

Limited to Municipal and Registered Primary and Secondary Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to municipal and registered private primary and secondary schools, stating that in accordance with the regulations established by the Ministry of Education for student graduation examinations in primary and secondary schools, students in the graduating classes of municipal and registered private primary schools, junior high schools, and senior high schools (general curriculum) in this semester should all hold graduation examinations. All regulations such as the organizational regulations of the graduation examination committee, the detailed rules of procedure, the methods of examination, and the methods of calculating grades have been separately formulated by the bureau and submitted to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government for approval. The examination methods and grade calculation methods should be published immediately. All schools handling graduation in this semester for primary, junior high, and senior high schools (general curriculum) must submit a roster of students taking the graduation examination by the end of April and a report of the students' academic, moral, and physical grades by May 20. Middle schools must also attach two 2.5-inch headshots of each student, with the school name, student name, and age marked on the back of the photo for verification. In addition to separate orders, this order is to be distributed urgently for compliance. This order.

Graduation Examination Methods 187

1. All students in the graduating classes of municipal and registered private primary schools, junior high schools, and senior high schools (general curriculum) in this city must participate in the examination. 2. The examination subjects are tentatively set as follows: A. Primary School: Chinese, Arithmetic, Social Studies, Nature, Physical Education. B. Junior High School: Party Principles, Chinese, Arithmetic, History, Geography, Nature, Physical Education, Foreign Language. C. Senior High School (General Curriculum): Party Principles, Chinese, Arithmetic, History, Geography, Physics, Chemistry, Biology, Foreign Language, Physical Education. However, for this session, the Physical Education grades may be strictly examined and reported by each school to the Examination Committee for verification.

2. The examination content of each subject is based on the Ministry's current curriculum standards, including all teaching materials studied in each stage, and is not limited to the teaching materials of the last semester.

3. One and a half months before the graduation examination for primary and secondary schools, each school should prepare a roster in the following format and submit it to the bureau for review. Secondary schools must also attach two 2.5-inch headshots of each student, with the school name, student name, and age marked for verification. (Note) If a school operates senior high, junior high, and primary school graduates at the same time, the students of the three grades should be listed separately in each roster.

4. The grades of each subject in the past three years for middle school students and the past two years for primary school students participating in the graduation examination, as well as their usual conduct grades and physical health status (all based on average grades), should be filled in separately by each school in the following form (form omitted) and reported to the bureau for filing half a month before the examination. (Note) If a school operates senior high, junior high, and primary school graduates at the same time, the students of the three grades should be listed separately in each form.

5. The examination questions for each subject are sealed by the chairman of the Examination Committee and handed over to the proctor, who will open them temporarily at the examination venue for use.

6. The proctors are appointed by the executive committee members of the primary, junior high, and senior high school groups of the Examination Committee. If there are not enough proctors when holding examinations in different districts, members of the Examination Committee may be added to serve as proctors.

7. The matters of invigilation and grading are handled separately by the members of the Examination Committee and assistant examiners.

8. All examination papers are sealed. After being sealed by the bureau, they are handed over to the proctor, who will open and distribute them separately at the examination venue. Examinees should only fill in the school and personal number assigned by the bureau on the examination paper.

9. After the examination of each subject is completed, the examination papers are sealed again by the proctor, stamped with a personal seal, and brought back to the bureau to be reviewed and scored separately by the Examination Committee. Then, the seals are opened to verify the names.

10. The seating arrangement for examinees is arranged by the bureau, with the principle of mixed distribution and complete isolation.

11. The locations and dates of the primary and secondary school examinations are determined by the Examination Committee.

12. If a student fails one subject in the examination, they will not be allowed to graduate. If they fail one or two subjects, they may retake the failed subjects once. If they still fail the retake, they will be allowed to make up the course for one academic year and participate in the examination of the relevant subjects at the next examination, but only once. Those who fail three or more subjects should be required to repeat the grade, but repeating the grade is also limited to once. 14. The date for the re-examination of failed subjects will be determined separately by the bureau.

13. Students who are supposed to participate in the graduation examination but cannot take the examination temporarily due to illness or special circumstances may be allowed by each school to apply to the bureau for a re-examination or make-up examination at the next examination.

14. At the end of the examination, in addition to posting the grades of the students and the grades of the schools, the bureau will also prepare various grade reports in accordance with the following table format and submit them to the Ministry of Education for filing. (Table omitted)

15. Examination instructions and examination rules will be formulated by the Examination Committee. 18. These methods will be implemented after being submitted to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government for approval and filing.

Grade Calculation Methods 188

(1) Grade calculation uses the percentage method as the standard. Decimals below integers are rounded to the nearest integer. 80 to 100 points is grade A, 70 to 79 points is grade B, 60 to 69 points is grade C, 50 to 59 points is grade D, and less than 50 points is grade E. A, B, and C are passing grades, and D and E are failing grades.

(2) Calculate the percentage of each subject in the total examination time of each subject in primary school based on the time taught each week in each subject. Multiply the percentage by the examination score of each subject, and then add them together and divide by 100 to get the overall average score. For example, as follows:

Primary School Grade Calculation Method

Subject | Teaching Time Per Week | Score | Percentage | Examination Score | Percentage Multiplied by Actual Score

---|---|---|---|---|---

Chinese | 390 | | 44.80 | 50 | 22.40

Arithmetic | 180 | | 20.70 | 60 | 12.42

Social Studies | 150 | | 17.25 | 70 | 12.07

Nature | 150 | | 17.25 | 60 | 10.35

Total | 870 | | 100 | 240 | 57.24

(3) The method of calculating grades in junior high and senior high schools (general curriculum) is based on the temporary curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education. The percentage of the total credits of each subject in the sum of the total credits of each subject for three academic years is multiplied by the score obtained in this examination and added together to get the average of the student's overall grade. For example, as shown in the following table:

Junior High School Grade Calculation Method

Subject | Examination Score | Credits | Percentage | Examination Score Multiplied by Percentage | Each Subject's Score

---|---|---|---|---|---

Party Principles | A | 12 | 0.08 | A |

Chinese | B | 36 | 0.24 | B |

History | C | 12 | 0.08 | C |

Geography | D | 12 | 0.08 | D |

Arithmetic | E | 30 | 0.21 | E |

Natural Science | F | 15 | 0.10 | F |

Foreign Language | G | 30 | 0.21 | G |

Total | | X = Overall Average

Senior High School (General Curriculum) Grade Calculation Method

Subject | Examination Score | Credits | Percentage | Examination Score Multiplied by Percentage | Each Subject's Score

---|---|---|---|---|---

Party Principles | A | 6 | 0.05 | A |

Chinese | B | 24 | 0.21 | B |

Arithmetic | C | 18 | 0.16 | C |

History | D | 12 | 0.10 | D |

Geography | E | 6 | 0.05 | E |

Physics | F | 8 | 0.07 | F |

Chemistry | G | 8 | 0.07 | G |

Biology | H | 8 | 0.07 | H |

Foreign Language | I | 26 | 0.22 | I |

Total | | 116

(4) The physical education grade is strictly examined by each school and reported separately, and is not averaged with other subjects.

(5) These methods will be implemented after being submitted to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government for approval and filing.

216-Kilometer Shanghai-Hangzhou Long-Distance Race Starts This Morning 199

An Unprecedented Feat by the Baihong Track and Field Team

Starting at Chen YingShi Tower at 8:00 AM

A Total of Eighteen Athletes Participating

The unprecedented 216-kilometer Shanghai-Hangzhou long-distance race, initiated by the Baihong Track and Field Team, will start at 8:00 AM this morning at Chen YingShi Tower in Ximen. A total of eighteen athletes are participating. It is expected that they will arrive at the bronze statue of Chen YingShi on the West Lake within four days, marking a grand beginning to a new era in Chinese sports.

Baihong Declaration 200

In the past, we have often seen long-distance races held in foreign countries, from one city to another, taking seven or eight days or more than ten days, covering six or seven hundred or more than a thousand miles. The scale is grand and truly sufficient to demonstrate the spirit of martial valor. I secretly admired it. Looking back at China's sports undertakings, they seem to rise and fall, seeming to be invigorated and seeming to decline. It is not easy to ask those in power to organize this kind of long-distance running. Although those in power are difficult to expect, it is not hopeless to spontaneously rise up, plan, and carry out. Since the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway was recently built, the long distance is a place for heroes to show their skills. The desire to try among colleagues is even more unstoppable. Therefore, we consulted with all parties and were fortunate to receive support. This long-distance run can be observed, which will make a considerable contribution to sports in our country. It is our hope that all participating athletes will strive to achieve this.

Staff List 201

Starter: Shen Siliang; Head Referee: Lao Jieming; Referees: Kang Yong, Sun Duoqi, Yu Cunyao; Timekeeping Referee and Disciplinarian: Chen Baolin, Zhu Jianshu; Accommodation Logistics: Kang Yong, Lao Jieming, Sun Duoqi, Zhu Jianshu; First Aid: Chen Baolin, Zhu Jianshu,

Participating Athletes 202

In addition to the Baihong team members participating, athletes from Hangzhou Changzhou (Zhongda Cao Chengjin and Jiang Wensen sent letters stating that they could not spare time due to the school's upcoming sports meet) have also signed up. Apart from two or three who dared not try, almost all of the long-distance running experts in East China are present, which can be described as a beautiful gathering of hosts and guests from Southeast China. The names are listed below: (1) Wu Shuying (2) Chen Xuzhou (3) Kuang Shihuai (4) Li Yage (5) Lin Quanbo (6) Bao Yibi (7) Zhou Ruquan (8) Xu Yanbo (9) Bai Zilong (10) Chai Huanjin (11) Zhu Shengyuan (12) Huang Shengbai (13) He Dafu (14) Jin Zhongkang (15) Zhou Wangqian (16) Wu Xun (17) Meng Guangyi (18) Xie Guolue

Four-Day Route 203

Day 1: The entire course is 216 kilometers. Today, depart at 8:00 AM from Chen Yingshi Memorial Tower in Lao Ximen, via Zhonghua Road, Huangjia Que Road, Chezhan Road, Coal Cinder Road, Xietu Road, and onto the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, via Minhang, Nanqiao, Zhaolin, Beiku, and to Caojing, totaling approximately 58,000 meters, which must be completed within eight hours.

Day 2: Tomorrow, depart from Caojing, via Jinshanzui, Jinshanwei, Jin Siniang Bridge, Jin Gongting Town, Xingxing Town, Niuqiao City, Zhapu, Qianchang, Wutuan, and to Haiyan, totaling approximately 58,000 meters, which must be completed within eight hours.

Day 3: Sunday, depart from Haiyan, via Changchuan Dam, Ganpu, Jiaoliyan, Huangwan Town, Zhakou, Xincang Town, Babao, and to Haining, totaling approximately 54,000 meters, which must be completed within seven and a half hours. Day 4: Monday, depart from Haining, via Hujia Dou, Yuanjia Ba, Wengjia Bu, Qiaosi, Qibao, enter Hangzhou through Qingtai Gate, walk Cheng Zhan Da Ma Lu, Dongjie Lu, Xinmin Lu, Yingzi Lu, Hubin Lu, and the finish line is at the bronze statue of Chen Yingshi on Hubin, totaling approximately 44,000 meters, which must be completed within six hours.

Donations 204

The budget for this event is 400 yuan. Currently, Mr. Zeng has donated 200 yuan, an anonymous person has donated 50 yuan, and Mr. Lou Zuyi and Mr. Shen Yangyi have jointly donated 40 yuan. The remaining amount is still being raised. The deficit will be supplemented from the team's regular expenses.

Important Rules 205

(1) The starting time each day is 8:00 AM; (2) The decision on whether to proceed in case of rain shall be made by the head referee, and the athletes shall not object; (3) Athletes shall not take vehicles or seek assistance from others during the race, otherwise, their right to participate will be revoked; (4) Athletes are not allowed to have accompanying runners along the way; (5) The staff will arrange for proper accommodation and food, and the athletes shall not arbitrarily protest; (6) Athletes shall not get into the ambulance midway, regardless of the circumstances. Anyone who gets into the ambulance will be disqualified; (7) Athletes should always demonstrate the spirit of sportsmanship; (8) The winning result will be calculated based on the total time spent for the entire course (i.e., the total time spent each day); (9) On the last day, from Haining to Hangzhou, the first to reach the finish line will receive an additional silver shield; (10) Those who cannot continue before reaching Haiyan must take a long-distance bus back to Shanghai at their own expense; (11) Those who cannot continue after Haiyan will have their travel expenses back to Shanghai provided by the team, but all actions shall be under the command of the team; (12) If an athlete fails to run within the specified time once during the trip, it will be deemed that they cannot continue and will not be able to continue participating in the race.

Spring and Autumn

Peach Blossoms and Literature 206

— Zhan Lu

The peach blossom is a pure folk writer. It especially likes to adorn the scenery for the people of humble dwellings. It always happily paints and depicts places that the aristocratic writer peony and the bureaucratic writer peony disdain to look at. Passersby on the road, seeing the colors of its writing, will happily forget their own toil. All contemporary men of letters especially bring wine to appreciate its folk literature. This shows that its great works truly have value that can be appreciated by both the refined and the vulgar. Moreover, in summer and autumn, the conclusion of its writing is always so sweet that people cannot bear to let it go.

Someone said: "The peach blossom is a writer who submits one manuscript to four different places. It can only create this one article, but the places where it is published are four different places, either on the tree, in the air, on the ground, or on the water. Although the locations are different, the materials are the same. Isn't this submitting one manuscript to four different places?" I said: Not so. Although the materials are the same, there are four articles. The one it writes on the tree is so splendid and colorful, like fire and tea. The one written in the air, "It will fly again as a whirling wind dance, already falling still presenting half a face makeup," how heavenly and ethereal! The one written on the ground, contrasting with the emerald green ground cover, how scattered and embellished, everywhere becomes a profound truth. The one written on the water, "Flowing water and falling flowers, spring is gone, heaven and earth," how touching and evocative, tying people's dreams? The ancients admired its writing, only admiring the one written on the water, calling it "Falling flowers on the water are all writing." In fact, its four articles are all good, and the one written on the water is especially its masterpiece of "that turn of the eye before leaving."

Trivial News of Liang Shiyi's Death 207

— Yong

Liang Shiyi's death has been reported previously. It is now heard that Chinese and foreign acquaintances have been coming to pay their respects in an endless stream, because Liang had extremely wide social connections during his lifetime. His family, because Liang had been living in a foreign country and was often depressed, plans to have a memorial service in Shanghai and then transport the coffin back to Guangdong, without going to Hong Kong again. Also, the funeral ceremony will strictly follow his grandfather's teachings, without using drums and music, without using monks and Taoists, not choosing auspicious days, and using extremely simple methods in everything to correct customs, it is said.

Before Liang went north, he wrote a poem, saying: "Snowy hair stroked, the midday dream is broken, plum blossoms on the riverbank and willows look the same, five thousand miles away are twin granddaughters, forty years ago I was an old historian, not showing off my writing to amaze the world, only leaving my blood to be sprinkled on the riverbank, cheering the group of younger brothers to sharpen their long swords, looking far at the New Pavilion, wanting to take the saddle." At that time, the atmosphere on the border was already bad, and Liang wanted to go to Peiping with some plans, so his words said so. What he called "leaving my blood to be sprinkled on the riverbank" was considered strange by many readers, but now he died on the Huangpu Riverbank, also a poetic premonition. Liang wrote very few poems in his life, and this is his last poem, it is said.

Liang's family finances are not very abundant, not as rumored outside, but all his sons are able to support themselves with a skill. Recently, related parties have discussed sending condolences, but his family plans to transfer them to public welfare memorial purposes, and the specific method will be discussed in detail by relatives and friends, it is said.

Liang had a very close private friendship with Duan Zhigui and Tang Shaoyi because of the Xinhai Revolution. Duan, hearing of Liang's death, repeatedly sent people to express condolences while ill. Tang Shaoyi sent a telegram from Guangdong, expressing his grief, and will personally send a eulogy portrait to Shanghai, it is said.

Returning Goose from the North 208

— Liang Ying

Qi Ge:

The fleeting time, since I quietly left Shanghai and went north stealthily, has been almost a month. Half a month ago, I mailed a brief note telling you fragments of my life, and in theory, you should have received it earlier!

Our organization has now been renamed the "Liao Ji Hei People's Support ×× Team". Although I am still in training, the work is also very intense: four hours of strict training, two hours of sentry duty, and a 30-mile run are the fixed routine every day. Two meals a day of sorghum and cabbage have created my strong muscles and determined will! The bugle calls in the army constantly spread out tragic tones! I am excited. I feel that only military life makes me excited!

"Recently, Song's army won an unprecedented victory in the Battle of Xifengkou, killing over ten thousand enemies and recovering territory for a hundred miles..." When this news reached our team, the whole team cheered like thunder. An excited and tense atmosphere permeated the entire

Newly Appointed Star Zhang Yanqing as the Thirteenth Sister (Presented by the Owner of the Plum Blossom Hall)

drill ground! Our red blood is surging, our muscles are twitching! The captain raised his thumb and said loudly: "Brothers, we will definitely have such a day! ..." Of course, we are constantly eager to kill the Japanese devils with our own hands and shed blood on the battlefield! We will use fresh blood to wash away our humiliation! We will use our heads to exchange for 　　who knew that when I walked to the accounting department of the newspaper office, the window opening, which was a foot high and half a foot wide, although not crowded with people, was squeezed with six or seven fellow contributors. Tall, short, fat, thin, Western suits and leather shoes, long gowns and short jackets, all styles were available, all kinds were complete. There was also a Miss Cao ××, the daughter of Father Jin Shenfu Road, (or perhaps she was), also squeezed in the crowd to collect manuscript fees for Mr. Cao. I knew a little about the civilization brought by the foreign adults, so I immediately stood behind Miss Cao. Then came another one, two, three, the former had not left, the latter came again, everyone holding a payment slip in their hands. Small slips, one after another, looked like porridge tickets for relieving hungry people.

Everyone lengthened their necks, waiting for the opening, the first one wanted to go to the toilet, the second one was impatient and would come back later, the third one..., so that those standing behind could get to the front earlier. But this was wishful thinking, just like hoping for a major earthquake in Japan to automatically abandon the Northeast, like a blind man hoping for the sky to collapse. In this tense atmosphere where everyone's hot sweat rolled from their foreheads all the way to their waists, footsteps thudded, and another university student-style comrade joined this group of people. Suddenly, this comrade discovered that the second person standing outside the opening was an old friend, went forward to shake hands, squeezed their shoulder, and cut in line to be the third person. Fortunately, these comrades were all civilized, so everyone stepped back one position and waited patiently.

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 209

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Four: The Affair Rekindles in the Teahouse, Accumulated Feelings Pour Out; the Year-End is Difficult to Endure, the Pawnshop Utters Mournful Cries.

Gui Zhi stirred the lotus root powder with a small teaspoon, scraping around the surface, taking a little bit and sending it to her mouth, smiling and lifting her shoulder, then lowering her eyelids and humming, "You're definitely lying." Ji Zhi hurriedly looked at her and asked, "What have I lied about?" Gui Zhi said, "Didn't you say at my house the other day that you were going to teach the servants a lesson? How come now you say you don't dare to offend the servants and maids at all?" These words immediately put Ji Zhi in an extremely awkward position, and he had to chuckle for a while before nodding his head and saying, "Your question is very reasonable. But that day, I was really angry. It's not a lie that I said in front of you that I would go back and teach them a lesson." Gui Zhi said, "Then that day, you must have given the servants and maids a big lesson when you went back." After saying that, she chuckled. Ji Zhi said, "You naturally understand, I can't scold them too much, because they're not using my money and working for me." Gui Zhi laughed and said, "Then you scolded them a little." Ji Zhi said, "But after my investigation, I can't blame the servants either. How would they dare to offend the neighbors?" Gui Zhi said, "I said that day that without orders from above, the people below wouldn't dare to act recklessly, but you always had to cover up for the people in your mansion. Now, this is news that you yourself have revealed." Ji Zhi said, "I admit that I'm very sorry to you, but I can't help it, you should forgive me." Gui Zhi continued to slowly eat the lotus root powder, but didn't pay attention to Ji Zhi's words. Seeing that she still didn't show any sign of forgiveness, Ji Zhi sighed for no reason. Seeing that he looked unhappy, Gui Zhi then asked, "Why are you sighing again?" Ji Zhi said, "Why shouldn't I sigh? We've been neighbors for a year now. You know what kind of attitude I've had over the past year. Now, just because of a little misunderstanding, you don't trust me to this extent." Gui Zhi said, "I don't have any reason to distrust you!" She said, then smiled slightly. Ji Zhi said, "How much more distrust do you want? You don't believe anything I say, thinking that I'm lying to you in front of you. I only have... "As he said this, he looked at Gui Zhi, hesitated for a while, and then stammered, "If I had some money in hand now and could start a small family, I would proceed... Then you would trust me." (41)

Glory! We want to draw out the Japanese sinews, peel off their skin, eat their flesh, and suck their blood; drive all the Japanese devils out of our territory and drink the Yellow Dragon in the shortest period of time!

Indeed, our hometown is lovely: there are kind parents, loving siblings, and close friends... But, now I feel that our country is even more lovely! We should cherish our country above all else! The country is the lifeline of the people, and the people are the soul of the country...

It's time for evening exercises, goodbye! Xiang wrote on March 29th in Xizhimen, Peiping (Transfer payment to the Aviation Association)

Collecting Manuscript Fees 210

— Xian Xian

After writing manuscripts for a month, pouring out my heart and soul, I waited eagerly for the end of the month. I respectfully wrote a payment slip. Without asking the seal official to stamp it, I grabbed my own seal, used all my strength to stamp it, and took off with my flying legs, taking two steps in three, straight to Wangping Street. All the way, I calculated, last month's performance was good, I might not get five yuan for manuscript fees, but four yuan, ninety-nine cents, I wouldn't get a cent less. This month, a pair of shoes, three pairs of socks, would be taken care of. With the extra, I could eat two meals of Russian cuisine. At least it would be foreign flavor.

Social Realism

Sampan 211

— Yiqiu from Wuxi

This place is full of the vitality of ordinary people. Sampans that are generally drifting along are constantly gathering here. Their lives are so casual and sacred! Everyone must use their own strength to feed themselves, except for young children who cannot walk yet. Ah! The pride of the era!

Recently, a very dilapidated sampan came to the riverbank in front of our door. The male owner of this boat is a rickshaw puller, considered the most lowly in society. The female owner is also a woman worker who smashes stones, invisible to the eyes of adults and gentlemen. They have a thirteen- or fourteen-year-old son who brings a basket of pancakes and fried dough sticks to sell everywhere every morning, an eleven- or twelve-year-old daughter who goes to the factory every day to pick up coal cinders, and an eight- or nine-year-old daughter who glues and folds various red and green paper toys on the boat, preparing them for her brother to sell. Her part-time job is to lead a three-year-old brother and take care of the house. The sampan is truly a family of strength like them, the most modern family.

Yesterday, I happened to be walking with my wife Zhiyun at the door when I saw them gathered on the narrow stern of the boat, enjoying the fruits of their labor with their blood and sweat - green vegetables - snails - rice.

"These people are really suffering!" Zhiyun noticed their rice bowls and sighed to me. "I think there are probably very few people happier than them!" I replied. "You're talking nonsense again!" She seemed to be blaming me.

After a moment of silence:

"Oh, look how dirty their bedding is!" She seemed to have forgotten my nonsense and whispered to me. "Dirty? I think it's cleaner than those concubines in big mansions!" I smiled. She said I was talking nonsense, disliked me, she went inside, so I chatted with the male owner, the rickshaw puller, again: "A Gui! How many years have you been pulling a rickshaw?"

"Only been pulling for more than a year!"

"What did you do before?"

"Pushing a cart! Working as a dock worker!"

"Why didn't you pull a rickshaw before?"

"Our lives are uncertain. When we hear that a place is better, we move there. There's no need to move a car, and there's no need for coolies to move a car, because our home - the sampan - is very convenient to move back and forth. And we have the strength to do anything, so we don't have to identify one line to do. For example, in Shanghai, because there are many trams and buses, pulling a rickshaw is not profitable, I'll work as a dock worker. This year, coming here to pull a rickshaw, business is not bad!"

"Then how much money can you make a day now?"

"Excluding the rickshaw rent, I can make one or two strings of cash every day!"

"How much money can your wife earn smashing stones every day?"

"She can't do it, at most five or six hundred cash a day!"

"How much can your son earn selling pancakes a day?"

"A hundred cash!"

"How much money can your daughter sell for picking up coal cinders?"

"Coal cinders are used to cook rice, not sold for money!"

"How much can your little daughter earn making paper figures a day?"

"At most one or two hundred cash!"

"How much rice does your family eat every day?"

"Always five or six liters!"

"And miscellaneous expenses?"

"We are poor people and don't have any miscellaneous expenses. We don't even drink tea. The only things we can't save on are soap and haircuts, which average one or two yuan a month, which is enough!"

"Then your income is enough to cover your expenses! Do you have any surplus every day?"

"As it stands now, we can have more than one string of cash surplus every day!"

"How do you use the surplus money?"

"Prepare to add some clothes or make up for it when business is bad!"

Night fell, the earth gradually darkened, and our conversation also ended. I was happy because I discovered one corner of life that people never pay attention to, and moreover, it is an unexpectedly happy family.

Free Talk

The Chinese People's Life Circle 212

— He Jia Gan

"Even ants know how to cherish life," and Chinese people have always called themselves "ant people." For the sake of temporarily preserving my own life, I often pay attention to relatively safe places. Apart from heroes and outstanding individuals, I presume no one would mock me for this.

However, I don't quite believe positive reports; I often look at things from a different perspective. For example, when the newspapers say that Peiping is preparing for air defense, I don't find it reassuring. But when I see antiques being transported south, I immediately sense the crisis of the ancient city and, from the whereabouts of these antiques, I infer the location of a Chinese paradise.

Now, batches of antiques are being concentrated in Shanghai, indicating that the safest place is still the Shanghai International Settlement.

However, rents are bound to rise.

This is also a major blow to the "ant people," so we still need to think of other places.

After much deliberation, I thought of a "life circle." That is to say, it's neither the "hinterland" nor the "border," but something in between, like a ring or a circle. In this place, one might be able to "eke out a living in troubled times."

On the "border," airplanes drop bombs. According to Japanese newspapers, they are "剿滅" (exterminating) "soldier bandits"; according to Chinese newspapers, they are slaughtering the people, leaving villages and markets in ruins. In the "hinterland," airplanes also drop bombs. According to Shanghai newspapers, they are "剿滅" (exterminating) "communist bandits," who are being bombed to pieces. What do the "communist bandits'" newspapers say? We don't know. But in short, on the border, it's bomb, bomb, bomb; in the hinterland, it's also bomb, bomb, bomb. Although on one side, it's others bombing, and on the other, it's ourselves bombing, the bombers are different, but the bombed are the same. Only in the space between these two, as long as the bombs don't accidentally fall down, there is still hope of avoiding "flesh and blood flying everywhere." Therefore, I call it the "Chinese People's Life Circle."

If bombs come from outside, this "life circle" will shrink into a "life line"; if more bombs come, everyone will flee into the already bombed "hinterland," and this "life circle" will end as a "life zero."

In fact, everyone has this premonition. Just look at how, in the past year, we no longer see the cliché "China has a vast territory, abundant resources, and a large population" in articles. That's one piece of evidence. And one gentleman even said in a speech that Chinese people are a "weak nation."

But the big shots don't think so, because they not only have airplanes but also their "foreign country"!

On National Language 213

— Lin Yutang

"National Language" is the shortened form of "Chinese people's language." For Chinese people, it's unnecessary to say the word "Chinese" because everyone already understands. Speaking this way, the term "National Language" is different from other foreign languages, and its meaning is similar to "National Medicine," "National Scolding," and "National Food," where the focus is on the word "National." Therefore, what resembles the language of Chinese people is "National Language," and what doesn't is not. For example, when Feng Yuxiang once sent a telegram scolding Wu Zhihui as a "hoary-bearded old thief, white-haired rascal," we felt that this wasn't "National Language" because it didn't sound like how Chinese people would speak and didn't fit the style of Chinese telegrams. When Zhang Xueliang sent a telegram resigning, saying, "The day I'm alive is the year I'll repay the country," we read it and thought it sounded like Chinese people would say, so it was proper "National Language."

I've often said that what is called "通" (tōng - fluent) in Chinese is what is called "idiomatic" in Western languages. "通" (tōng) is not just about being fluent, but about conforming to language habits, which isn't just a matter of grammar. Anything that conforms to Chinese grammar or language habits is called "通" (tōng). For example, in the Spring and Autumn Annals, "夏，享公" (Xia, Xiang Duke), even though there's no subject, it can still be considered "通" (tōng) because it conforms to language habits. Also, when Duke of Wei, Qin Hui, negotiated peace by ceding land, he wrote an amnesty to the Henan state army. Wuturu thought the "National Language" was not fluent because he did not elaborate upon the Great Jin's virtues. So, Hui ordered Cheng Kejun to write: "The heavens regret the disaster, fulfilling the spirits' wish to govern with peace of mind; the great nation practices benevolence, fulfilling the filial piety of children to their parents. This can be called a most grand occasion. How dare we forget the deep kindness that must be repaid..." Thereupon, Wuturu thought this was very fluent "National Language" because phrases like "benevolence," "filial piety," "grand occasion," and "deep kindness" all conform to Chinese language habits.

A country's language is where a country's cultural elites entrust their thoughts, so each can express its distinct national spirit. In China, due to special circumstances, reading became the exclusive privilege of a special class, so writing became even more ingenious, and the meaning of "writing" became particularly unique. It generally has the meaning of ornate writing, something orderly and colorful is called writing. Therefore, only Chinese has the term "文章" (wén zhāng - writing). The Western term "Belles-Lettres" is still far from the meaning of "文章" (wén zhāng - writing). For example, "不抵抗" (bù dǐ kàng - non-resistance) is plain speech, but "長期抵抗" (cháng qī dǐ kàng - long-term resistance) has literary flourish and is writing. "不攘外" (bù rǎng wài - don't expel the foreigners) is plain speech, but "先安内" (xiān ān nèi - first pacify the interior) has literary flourish and is writing. This kind of "National Language" is something foreign languages don't have. As for military men suddenly wanting to fight, they must also "師出有名" (shī chū yǒu míng - have a justified cause) or comfort the people or punish the guilty. When their memorial to the throne is written well, if it is coherent, eloquent, and meaningful, scholars will eagerly spread it and praise it. The only ones who don't understand and are fooled are the common people who don't know the meaning and rules of writing.

Here are three things to know about writing "National Language":

(1) Indirect Expression: Mencius said that expressing oneself clearly is the essence of writing, the true way, and unchanging for all time. However, this can only be said for sages and wise people. Because clarity is wonderful, but we are not sages, and what we want to express may be ordinary. Therefore, mere clarity cannot be writing; it must be embellished with literary flourish. Therefore, Xunzi went a step further, advocating "曲得所謂" (qū dé suǒ wèi - obtaining the desired effect indirectly). The "Non-Physiognomy" chapter says, "Gentlemen are never tired of speaking, but the vulgar are the opposite, liking the substance but not caring about the style, so they can never avoid being base and vulgar." The writing of Mozi's followers, for example, is like liking the substance but not caring about the style. Because they don't care about the style, right and wrong are clear, but there is no beauty of "曲得所謂" (qū dé suǒ wèi - obtaining the desired effect indirectly), so they are vulgar for life. The vulgar cannot write "deeply worded and comprehensively inclusive" articles.

(2) Withholding: Barbarians who go to war capture one and eat one. They never have what is called "desiring to capture, therefore releasing," so they never enjoy the glory of Meng Huo being captured seven times. The tactics of capturing and releasing in warfare are the tactics of withholding in writing. The commentator thought that Feng Yuxiang's words, quoted above, were too blunt and lacked restraint. Feng suffered from this because he did not know the importance of withholding. Speaking exhaustively invites blame. There is a clear saying of ancient times, so those who are good at writing must not speak exhaustively, leaving something unfinished for future meetings. Therefore, writing must use more words like "however," "then also," "if," and "may also." As the poem says, "Turn it left, turn it left, the gentleman is suited; turn it right, turn it right, the gentleman possesses it." If it's suitable on the left and possessed on the right, it will have endless benefits in the future, and this is the gentleman.

(3) Lightness: Writing should avoid haste, revealing, and blurting out, as mentioned above. But to avoid haste and revealing, one must first cultivate the mind and nature, read ten thousand books, and have an open mind, which is called cultivation. Words are the voice of the heart, so to write Chinese people's language, one must first have a Chinese person's heart. Therefore, writing must first cultivate life, raise geese, plant chrysanthemums, watch clouds, and appreciate the moon, so that the heart is light. Then, looking at oneself, worldly affairs are like floating clouds, and reclaiming the Northeast is good, and giving away the four provinces is fine too. At this point, one can then lightly extend the wrist, and casually hold the writing brush between the thumb and middle finger; not fast, not slow, not heavy, not light, relying on the contact between the brush and the white paper, quietly writing out one word at a time, like watching a fire from across the river, commenting on right and wrong, debating without arguing, observing without getting excited, not left, not right, 母適, 母必 (do not force, do not insist), like war and like peace, like sunny and like rainy. Leftists read it as tragic, rightists read it as gentle, and adding a couple of sentences from Wang Yangming's "cultivating the mind" will make it very elegant.

These three methods: indirect expression can also be called the "setting off the moon with clouds" method, withholding can also be called the "dragon turning, phoenix dancing" method, and lightness can also be called the "watching the fire from across the river" method. When the work of these three methods is refined, one becomes a Chinese literati.

Suffering 214

— Jiang Tianwei

This is one of the most unforgettable things in my childhood. This tragic scene is forever etched on my heart. The more I try to forget it, the clearer it appears.

I was nine years old then, and my younger brother was only six years old. My older brother was three years older than me. That year, there was a drought, and there was often not a single grain of rice in the house, and naturally no money either. Father had already gone out. Mother and Grandmother often whispered to each other, with tears in their eyes, looking so pained.

One day, I heard Mother say to Grandmother:

"We absolutely can't let the three children eat like that, and Mom can't eat like that either. Only I..."

I didn't understand why Mother said that. "I can't eat?" What couldn't she eat? I was suspicious.

"Let me suffer! When their father comes back, there will always be some money for us, even if it's just a dime. Now, I can only keep doing this..." As Mother said this, more tears flowed. Grandmother also wept.

I was a sensitive and melancholic child. Seeing Mother and Grandmother so sad, I felt very uncomfortable. I didn't know what they were sad about, and I didn't dare to ask. At dinner, Mother brought us four bowls of porridge. My older brother and younger brother swallowed their bowls of porridge quickly without thinking. I pretended that the porridge was too hot and ate slowly. Grandmother also ate slowly like me. I thought of what Mother had said during the day, and I seemed to understand a little. I couldn't help calling out in a sad voice:

"Mother! Mother! Come and eat!"

"I've already eaten!" Mother replied from the kitchen, her throat sounding like it was stuffed with something. "Kui'er! Eat well!" Grandmother said to me gently.

I really couldn't bear it. Why didn't Mother come and eat with us? I put down my bowl and ran to the kitchen. I wanted Mother to come and eat with us. When I ran into the kitchen, Mother was struggling to swallow something, and she hid it as soon as she saw me.

"Mom will come and eat with you soon. I still have something to finish, and then I'll come!"

Mother, with a pained expression, followed me and sat down at the table.

Grandmother still hadn't swallowed her bowl of thin porridge. When she saw Mother, she couldn't hold back her sorrow and shed a few old tears, but Mother remained silent.

I saw that Mother's mouth had many bran-like crumbs on it. My child's heart felt like it had suddenly received a heavy blow, and I immediately started crying. Mother and Grandmother had no idea why I was crying.

After that, I followed Mother at all times, except when I went up the mountain to chop firewood.

Crossroads of the Times and Love 215

— Zhang Ziping

Everyone responded together. What a tragic and stirring moment! Then, they shouted a few more moving slogans and moved forward northwards. Haiquan saw a streetcar coming, so he hid behind the streetcar and scattered some leaflets on the Baidu Bridge, shouting slogans with incorrect pronunciation. Later, he just echoed their shouts, yelling "Ah, ah" emptily. He was worried that police officers would come and catch him from the front and back. When he turned his head to look south, he saw Li Yixiang leading a few senior figures from the literary world following from a distance.

They finally crossed the Baidu Bridge. Usually, one could see two Scottish soldiers standing guard there with long guns, but fortunately, they weren't there today. They turned into North Suzhou Road and advanced westward along North Suzhou Road, shouting slogans and scattering leaflets.

"Oh no! This is terrible!"

They were about to approach the Zhapu Road Bridge. Haiquan saw a large group of black hounds coming from the front and back. Haiquan panicked and scattered all the leaflets in his hand into the Suzhou River. He paid attention to the movements of the hounds. Chinese people came forward to snatch their leaflets and banners. Two white officers came over to arrest the young people leading at the front. The Japanese were the most unreasonable, picking up wooden sticks and randomly hitting the legs of these young people. Haiquan circled around and hid at the entrance of a white Russian antique shop. He saw a short Japanese police officer being the most energetic, still waving the wooden stick in his hand and randomly beating a young man. Haiquan felt infinite pain seeing this. Suddenly, he heard a crash, and the Japanese police officer fell onto the road. It turned out that the poisonous beating of Chinese youth by the Japanese hound had angered a Chinese worker who had just walked by on the other side. He picked up the wine bottle in his hand and violently struck the side of the Japanese police officer's head. At that moment, another Japanese police officer fired a shot at the chivalrous worker. The worker fulfilled his glorious end in this way!

Haiquan felt that the loss from this demonstration was too great. Except for him and two other male comrades who escaped unscathed, it could be said that the entire army was wiped out. He felt that this sacrifice was too meaningless.

When he walked to the Seward Road intersection, he encountered a Japanese police officer who came to check his body. The police officer interrogated him in broken Shanghai dialect.

"I am seeing things!"

This was a Japanese sentence he had learned from Mrs. Tsuruko. He made use of it. The Japanese police officer smiled and let him pass.

Sitting in the streetcar, his chest was still pounding very hard. He secretly congratulated himself for having been so quick-witted just now, allowing him to escape the net. Otherwise, he would really be suffering at this moment. But on the other hand, he secretly cursed his own baseness and cowardice. He felt a contradictory pain.
